class="dpsp-total-share-count">58</span><span>shares</span></div></div><p>Knowledge is best shared. You might have heard this quote several times in life, and if you’ve ever shared your knowledge with someone you might know the feeling too. The more you share your knowledge, the greater the joy of having it becomes.</p><p>For learners, this shared knowledge can be of much help since one learns from wisdom more than anything else. Whether you realize it or not, you can learn far more from experts in your industry than in any other way.&nbsp;</p><p>All you need to do is find the right people in your niche. Just start by looking at the achievements of people and how they’ve got to a certain position. Self-made experts are the best to learn from because they can give you an insight into the real market and hardships that is one is bound to face. Moreover, you come to learn about smart strategies from their experience that is otherwise difficult to achieve.</p><p>Since internet marketing is a huge field, to begin with, you must always pick a specific niche that you want to master and go onto pursuing it by picking a guru. But don’t worry, if you’re having trouble finding the perfect Internet marketing ideal, to begin with. We’ve gone ahead and compiled the best of the best thought leaders and experts from the field of digital marketing that will help you become an expert in the field easily.&nbsp;</p><p>All of these gurus offer free materials in form or the other that can help you get started without having to burden yourself or paying for study material. So, here are the top 51 Internet marketing gurus in different expertise that you can look forward in 2020.</p><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-445205b ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-445205b-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-445205b-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Gary Vaynerchuk</h3><p>Born with an entrepreneurial spirit, Gary Vaynerchuk is the ultimate businessman. He is a proven investor and advisor in the world of startups across many countries. Gary is a master of the Fortune 500 world, online content marketing, social media among other things.</p></div><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-style-circle-mask"><img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 3" class="wp-image-33253" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1-100x100.jpg 100w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-lazy-src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1.jpg" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 3" class="wp-image-33253" srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/garyV-1-100x100.jpg 100w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px"></noscript></figure></div></div><p>He started thirty-three years ago by plucking flowers from other’s people yards in the neighborhood and selling them in the market. All that he learned from this experience was used by Gary to grow his wine store from $3 to $45 million in a span of a few years, by launching his website winelibrary.com.&nbsp;</p><p>Today Gary Vaynerchuk is the author of successful books, investor, motivator and chairman of VaynerX, which is a modern-day media and communication company. The current worth of Gary V is close to $ 200 million.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Resources from Gary V</strong></p><ul><li><a href="https://twitter.com/garyvaynerchuk?lang=en">Twitter</a></li><li>Website- <a href="http://garyvaynerchuk.com/">GaryVayerchuk.com</a></li><li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCctXZhXmG-kf3tlIXgVZUlw">Youtube</a></li><li><a href="https://www.garyvaynerchuk.com/podcast/">Podcast</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-3d60a7c ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-3d60a7c-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-3d60a7c-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Neil Patel</h3><p>The co-founder of Crazy Egg and Hello Bar, Neil Patel is a household name in the field of digital marketing. He helps organizations like Amazon, HP, GM, and Viacom grow their revenues. He has been ranked as the top influencer by the wall street journal, one of the top 10 online marketers by Forbes.</p></div><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-style-circle-mask"><img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 4" class="wp-image-33259" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1-100x100.jpg 100w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-lazy-src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1.jpg" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 4" class="wp-image-33259" srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/neilpatel-1-100x100.jpg 100w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px"></noscript></figure></div></div><p>His company has also made it to Entrepreneur Magazine’s top 100 most brilliant companies in the world. He is an expert in content marketing, social media marketing, lead generation etc. and authored several books in the niche. Neil started back at the age of 15 when he got his first job at Knotts Berry Farm, from where he went onto becoming a door to door marketer selling vacuums.&nbsp;</p><p>Soon Neil saved as much as $5000 and started his website Advice Monkey. He learned by trying and testing things to perfection. His net worth today is 7 to 10 million dollars.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Resources from Neil Patel</strong></p><ul><li><a href="https://twitter.com/neilpatel?ref_src=twsrc%5Egoogle%7Ctwcamp%5Eserp%7Ctwgr%5Eauthor">Twitter</a></li><li>Website- <a href="https://neilpatel.com/">neilpatel.com</a></li><li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCl-Zrl0QhF66lu1aGXaTbfw">Youtube</a></li><li><a href="https://marketingschool.io/all-episodes/">Podcast</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-55a5c11 ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-55a5c11-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-55a5c11-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Sam Ovens</h3><p>Yet another expert in the domain of digital marketing is Sam Ovens. He is Forbes 30 under 30 entrepreneur, founder of the Consuting.com and SnapInspect. His flagship venture Consulting accelerator has till now produced 25 millionaires along with other successful consultants.</p></div><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-style-circle-mask"><img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 5" class="wp-image-33262" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens-100x100.jpg 100w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-lazy-src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens.jpg" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 5" class="wp-image-33262" srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/samowens-100x100.jpg 100w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px"></noscript></figure></div></div><p>Sam landed his first job in Vodaphone at the age of 21, which is a dream come true for many people. But, he wanted to explore more and live the life of the riches. It was then that he decided to become an entrepreneur. His first venture failed miserably but he didn’t give up. Today, his net worth is as much as $65 million and is one of the best people out there who help organizations drive growth in their business using digital marketing strategies.</p><p><strong>Resources from Sam Ovens</strong></p><ul><li><a href="https://twitter.com/samovensnz?lang=en">Twitter</a></li><li>Website- <a href="https://www.consulting.com/sam-ovens">Consulting.com</a></li><li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC2wTiY8JLWNub751LN-5QvQ">Youtube</a></li><li><a href="https://www.podcasts.com/sam-ovens-podcast">Podcast</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-0ad71d3 ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-0ad71d3-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-0ad71d3-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Frank Kern</h3><p>Frank Kern is considered as one of the top Internet marketing gurus of all time. He is the creator of Behavioural Dynamic Response, which is an automated marketing method that can be used to speed up your sales cycle by customizing your marketing messages based on the behavior of your prospects.</p></div><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-style-circle-mask"><img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 6" class="wp-image-33252" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1-100x100.jpg 100w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-lazy-src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1.jpg" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 6" class="wp-image-33252" srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/frankkern-1-100x100.jpg 100w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px"></noscript></figure></div></div><p>Frank started in the year 1999, when he was fascinated by the way that the internet could be used to make money. But soon he discovered that making money from the Internet was not easy at all. He ventured into advertising and loved what he was doing.</p><p>When following Frank Kern, you can expect actionable strategies and tactics that can help market a business effectively, create blatant sales pitches and more. Frank Kern’s net worth is $35 million and he one of the best marketing consultants out there.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Resources from Frank Kern</strong></p><ul><li><a href="https://twitter.com/frank_kern?lang=en">Twitter</a></li><li>Website- <a href="https://frankkern.com/">Frankkern.com</a></li><li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/OfficialFrankKern">Youtube</a></li><li><a href="https://frankkern.com/podcast/">Podcast</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-884ad10 ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-884ad10-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-884ad10-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Seth Godin</h3><p>If you’ve even faintly heard about digital marketing, there are chances you might have not gone without hearing Seth Godin’s name. Seth is an American author, entrepreneur, marketer, public speaker among other things. He has established his thought leadership in the domain of digital marketing by writing 17 bestselling books, helping marketers and businesses from all across the world.</p></div><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-style-circle-mask"><img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%200%200'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 7" class="wp-image-33263" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1-100x100.jpg 100w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-lazy-src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1.jpg" alt="Top 70 Internet Marketing Gurus and Digital Marketing Experts 7" class="wp-image-33263" srcset="https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1.jpg 200w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1-180x180.jpg 180w, https://www.bloggingcage.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/sethgodin-1-100x100.jpg 100w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px"></noscript></figure></div></div><p>Seth Godin has more than a few online courses running on platforms like Udemy that have been taken by more than 60,000 people to date. He is an excellent teacher who started his career as a brand manager at the age of 23. From there, Seth went onto starting his own company called Seth Godin Production, which was a book packaging business.&nbsp;</p><p>However, it was in 1995, that Seth founded a company Yoyodyne that used innovative ideas to promote campaigns and target their audience.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Resources from Seth Godin</strong></p><ul><li><a href="https://twitter.com/ThisIsSethsBlog?ref_src=twsrc%5Egoogle%7Ctwcamp%5Eserp%7Ctwgr%5Eauthor">Twitter</a></li><li>Website- <a href="https://www.sethgodin.com/">sethgodin.com</a></li><li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BPK_qzeH_yk">Youtube</a></li><li><a href="https://seths.blog/podcasts/">Podcast</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-ugb-container ugb-container ugb-container--width-small ugb-8fb8193 ugb-container--v2 ugb-container--design-basic ugb-main-block" id=""><div class="ugb-inner-block"><div class="ugb-block-content"><div class="ugb-container__wrapper ugb-8fb8193-wrapper"><div class="ugb-container__side"><div class="ugb-container__content-wrapper ugb-8fb8193-content-wrapper"><div class="wp-block-columns"><div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%"><h3>Russell Brunson</h3><p>Russell Brunson is yet another Internet marketing guru who is also a serial entrepreneur and started his first online company, while he was still wrestling at the Boise State University.
